## 參考資料

<div class="references-small">

  - [](https://web.archive.org/web/20080705015955/http://galge.com/galge/nomember/brand/index.html)

<!-- end list -->

  - 曾製作成人遊戲的公司列表

<!-- end list -->

  - <http://erogamescape.dyndns.org/~ap2/ero/toukei_kaiseki/select.php>
    ＞SQL入力フォーム＞brandname from gamelist where erogame=true order by
    brandname＞実行
  - 或[1](http://erogamescape.dyndns.org/~ap2/ero/toukei_kaiseki/create_csv.php?SQL=SELECT+brandname+from+gamelist+where+erogame%3Dtrue+order+by+brandname)

<!-- end list -->

  - 排序

<!-- end list -->

  - <http://erogamescape.dyndns.org/~ap2/ero/toukei_kaiseki/select.php>
    ＞SQL入力フォーム＞id,brandname,url from brandlist order by id＞実行
  - 或[2](http://erogamescape.dyndns.org/~ap2/ero/toukei_kaiseki/create_csv.php?SQL=SELECT+id%2Cbrandname%2Curl+from+brandlist+order+by+id)
  - <http://erogamescape.dyndns.org/~ap2/ero/toukei_kaiseki/select.php>
    ＞SQL入力フォーム＞id,brandname,url from brandlist order by id＞実行
  - 或[3](http://erogamescape.dyndns.org/~ap2/ero/toukei_kaiseki/create_csv.php?SQL=SELECT+id%2Cbrandname%2Curl+from+brandlist+order+by+brandname)
